| v5.5.12 | **Uneven hero numeral heights fix (lining-nums)** — founder caught: the v5.5.11 hero "522" had the "5" visibly taller than the two "2"s. **Root cause**: Fraunces's default numeral style is **old-style figures** (`onum`) where some digits (5/7/9/3) are full-height with descenders while others (1/2/0) sit at x-height — so "522" shows a tall 5 next to two short 2s. Classic typography mistake when shipping a Fraunces hero number without explicitly forcing **lining-nums** (`lnum` — uniform-height numerals that align to the cap-height baseline). **Fix (scoped CSS, dg-system.css)**: `#rc-v2-num` adds `font-variant-numeric:lining-nums tabular-nums` (logical CSS) + belt-and-suspenders `font-feature-settings:"lnum","tnum"` (low-level OpenType for any older engine that doesn't fully implement the high-level property). Real-cert-app verify (computed-style ground truth): `fontVariantNumeric:"lining-nums tabular-nums"`, `fontFeatureSettings:'"lnum","tnum"'`, Fraunces-600 loaded, numerals visually uniform (5/2/2 same height). UAT **6381/6381** (no impact). Full local chromium Playwright per the locked discipline. **Lesson (locked)**: any Fraunces (or any old-style-default serif) hero numeral MUST explicitly request `lining-nums` if visual consistency across digits matters. tabular-nums alone only normalizes WIDTH, not figure-style. Same pattern applies to: any score/version/counter display in the Home/Analytics/Quiz/SR surfaces — re-audit if old-style ever reappears. Mandatory `dg-system.css?v` hand-bump 5.5.11→**5.5.12**. Fast-lane (CSS-only). |
| v5.5.11 | **Hero score overlap fix** — founder caught: the v5.5.10 "522" hero (Fraunces 140px) was overlapping the "OUT OF 900" caption — the "5" glyph curve dipped into the caption ink. **Root cause**: I copied `line-height:0.92` from the masthead concept (which used it for an inline `522 / 900` baseline-flex row where tight line-height keeps the row compact) — but on the v5.5.10 **block-stacked** hero where the caption sits directly underneath, a sub-1 line-height makes the glyph's ink-bottom extend BELOW the line-box, and Fraunces's "5" has a prominent curve that crossed into the 6px caption margin. **Fix (scoped CSS, dg-system.css)**: `#rc-v2-num` line-height `0.92 → 1.0` (gives the glyph its full natural line-box so ink stays inside), caption span margin-top `6px → 14px` (extra breathing room). Real-cert-app dual-theme verify (computed-style ground truth, the masthead's documented "trust computed over screenshots" pattern): `gap` between number bottom and caption top = **15px** (was 0/overlapping); both themes faithful. UAT **6381/6381** (value-only CSS, no guard impact). **Lesson (locked)**: when copying type-system values from one layout context to another, re-check `line-height` — values < 1.0 are safe for INLINE/baseline-flex rows but unsafe for BLOCK-stacked elements where the next element sits at the line-box bottom (the glyph's natural extents will overlap). Same class of mistake as the v5.5.4 portal `var(--dgh-ease)` issue — context determines what's valid. Mandatory `dg-system.css?v` hand-bump 5.5.10→**5.5.11**. Fast-lane (CSS-only; no DB/auth/money). |

| v5.5.6 | **Playwright CI-hang fix** (test-infra) — founder flagged "5.5.4 didn't go live." Investigation: the v5.5.4 gating run's Playwright step ran **~59 minutes then FAILED**; the gate never went green so `deploy-verification.yml` stayed red and v5.5.4/v5.5.5 never passed CI (they DID reach prod — Vercel's Git integration builds on direct push to `main` independently of the GitHub-Actions required check, which only blocks PR merges — so the *features* were live, but CI/branch-protection were broken and future PR merges blocked). **Root cause** (diagnosed, then reproduced + fixed + locally validated — not guessed): the v4.43.4 GLOBAL `test.beforeEach` force-opened `#custom-quiz-section` on **every** test (written when it was an inline collapsed `<details>` — harmless then). v5.5.4 turned that section into a portal modal (`position:fixed; inset:0; z-index:140`, scroll-locked, reparented to `<body>`). So post-v5.5.4 **every** test ran with a full-viewport modal backdrop over the page → the ~89 tests that don't touch the modal had their clicks intercepted → 30s actionability timeout + 1 retry each → ~59-min suite → failure. A second, smaller defect: 2 tests selected `#page-setup button:has-text("Generate Quiz")` but the portal moves that button OUT of `#page-setup` to `<body>`. **Fix (tests/e2e/app.spec.js only)**: (1) removed the GLOBAL force-open from the shared `beforeEach` (kept the Pro-tier `_certanvilSignedIn`/`_quotaState`/body-class stub — still required); (2) added a scoped `openCustomQuizModal` helper applied via `test.beforeEach(openCustomQuizModal)` to **only** the 4 modal-dependent describes (`Chip Selectors`, `API Key Validation`, `Default Chip Selections`, `Topic Chip Count`) — same DOMContentLoaded→`.open` mechanism as v4.43.4 but no longer global, so the backdrop never covers the ~89 tests that don't use it; (3) repointed the 2 Generate-Quiz selectors `#page-setup` → `#custom-quiz-section` (works whether the section is in `#page-setup` or portaled). **Local validation (the discipline v5.5.4/v5.5.5 skipped — the v4.99.74 "always run Playwright locally before push" lesson, re-learned the hard way)**: targeted chromium 14/14 in **8.7s** (previously-broken non-modal tests App Load 394ms / Theme Toggle 346ms now sub-second + all modal tests pass), then the **full chromium suite 99/99 in 1.5 min** (vs ~59 min → fail pre-fix). **4 fast-lane UAT tombstones** appended to the existing v4.99.32 Playwright-spec guard block (reuses its `e2eSpec`): scoped helper exists · applied ≥4× · the GLOBAL stub is NOT immediately followed by an open (the precise ~59-min-hang signature — caught in pre-commit seconds, not after an hour of hung CI) · the old global-open comment stays deleted. UAT **6377/6377** (6373 + 4). Class-of-bug-grep applied: the tombstone's own old-comment string is `+`-concatenated so it can't self-trip. No `dg-system.css?v` hand-bump (v5.5.6 changes no served CSS; the bump-version `sw.js` CACHE_NAME bump handles cache invalidation on the Vercel rebuild). Fast-lane per ENVIRONMENT_STRATEGY (test-infra + version bump; no DB/auth/money; sw.js = universal CACHE_NAME bump) → canonical trunk push; this push's CI exercises the fix and should finally go green, unblocking branch protection + deploy-verification. **Lesson (locked):** a render-path/DOM-relocation change (esp. a new overlay/modal) can silently break the *shared Playwright fixture* for the whole suite; UAT-green is not Playwright-green; run the full chromium suite locally before any push that touches a render path — and a long-running CI step that never flips is a *hang signature*, investigate it, don't wait it out. |

| v5.0.9 | HOTFIX — CSS parse failure: two truncated `cubic-bezier()` calls in `styles.css` silenced ~3,300 rules and broke all 9 Playwright 3D View tests. **Root cause**: `.acl-header-pill` (line 6150) and `.acl-tp-row` (line 6447) both had malformed `transition` values — `cubic-bezier(0.2,` with no closing `)`, just a trailing comma before the next property. The CSS parser kept consuming everything after each unclosed `(` as part of the function argument list, swallowing rule closers, selectors, and property declarations for the rest of the file. Among the casualties: `.tb-canvas-pills { position: absolute }`, all `.tb-pill` rules, palette/collapse-button positioning — everything the 3D View modebar needs to float above the canvas. Playwright found palette elements (`#tb-palette-collapse-btn`, `.tb-pane-rail-label`) intercepting pointer events at the 3D pill coordinates because the pill was `position: static` and `overflow: hidden`-clipped rather than floating. **Why brace-balance was misleading**: awk counts `{` and `}` as characters — balanced overall — but CSS parsing is function-context-aware; an unclosed `(` swallows `}` tokens as arguments. **Fix**: two lines changed — replaced `cubic-bezier(0.2,` truncated values with `cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)` (the standard ease-out curve used throughout the codebase). **Verified**: styles.css went from 2,656 parsed rules → 5,956/5,956. Playwright 3D View suite: 9 failing → 11/11 pass. Full suite: 101/101 Playwright chromium + 6334/6334 UAT. Temp diagnostic files `debug-positions.spec.js` + `debug-css-parse.spec.js` deleted. Fast-lane (two-line CSS fix + SW cache bump). |

cable wiring completion (if `tbPendingCableFrom` set and different device, syncs cable type via `tbSetSelectedCableType` then calls `tbAddCable`); otherwise starts drag (captures SVG offset, sets `_dragging` state, selects device via `tbSetSelectedId`). `_onMouseMove(e)` — drag handler: reads `_dragging.id`, finds device in `tbState.devices`, updates `dev.x`/`dev.y` with clamped position (55..TB_CANVAS_W-55, 45..TB_CANVAS_H-45), sets `_dragging.moved` flag on >3px delta, re-renders. `_onMouseUp(e)` — if `_dragging.moved` saves draft via `tbSaveDraft`; if not moved toggles cable pending mode (click same device again cancels, otherwise sets `tbPendingCableFrom`). `_onCanvasClick(e)` — deselects on empty canvas area (guards against device/cable targets). `_onCableClick(e)` — selects cable via `[data-v2-cable]` hitbox click. `_onPaletteDeviceClick(e)` — adds device via `tbAddDevice` at staggered center position (avoids stacking: offset by device count modulo). `_onCableChipClick(e)` — toggles cable type selection + syncs to V1 via `tbSetSelectedCableType`. `_attachKeyHandler()` — Delete/Backspace deletes selected via `tbDeleteSelected`, Escape clears selection + pending cable (guards against input/textarea/select focus). `_wireInteraction()` — master wiring fn called after engine load: SVG mousedown delegation, window mousemove/mouseup for drag, SVG click for deselect/cable-select, palette click delegation. `_updateStatus(msg)` — updates mode label with contextual feedback. **CSS** (`features/topology-builder-v2.css`): `.v2-device` `user-select:none` + `:active` cursor `grabbing`. 12 UAT guards (interaction handlers + V1 bridge mutations + state setters + double-click pattern). UAT **6311/6311**. Fast-lane (feature module changes only; no DB/auth/money; sw.js = universal CACHE_NAME bump). |

This is a **functional bug for Sec+ users**: they would see "Pass mark cleared · 720" when their real pass is 750, and a student scoring 730 would see a false pass verdict. **Sites fixed**: (1) `finish()` line 7605: `const passed = scaled >= 720` → `scaled >= EXAM_PASS_SCORE` (quiz flow pass/fail verdict logic); (2) `finish()` line 7620: verdict innerHTML `'↑ Pass mark cleared · 720'` → `'↑ Pass mark cleared · ' + EXAM_PASS_SCORE`; (3) `finish()` line 7624: `const gap = 720 - scaled` → `EXAM_PASS_SCORE - scaled` (below-pass gap calculation); (4) `submitExam()` line 8205: `'above the 720 pass mark'` → `'above the ${EXAM_PASS_SCORE} pass mark'` (exam result message — note: `submitExam` already used `EXAM_PASS_SCORE` for `const passed` at line 8114, but the DISPLAY STRING still said 720); (5) `showExamShortfallBanner()` line 6369: `'the 720 pass mark stays accurate'` → `'the ${EXAM_PASS_SCORE} pass mark stays accurate'`; (6-8) `MILESTONE_DEFS` lines 9151/9157/9177: `desc: 'Score 720+…'` → template literals `\`Score ${EXAM_PASS_SCORE}+…\`` for exam_pass, ready_720, and hardcore_pass milestones (note: the `MILESTONE_CHECKS` logic at lines 9423/9424/9430 was ALREADY using `EXAM_PASS_SCORE` — only the display descriptions were wrong); (9) readiness trajectory line 10502: `'(lower bound → 720)'` → `'(lower bound → ' + EXAM_PASS_SCORE + ')'`. **Class-of-bug**: the `EXAM_PASS_SCORE` constant was defined cert-aware from the start but 9 consumer sites never adopted it, hardcoding the Network+ value. The grep pattern was `\b720\b` across app.js — the fix is to use the constant everywhere. Remaining `720` references verified CORRECT: line 104 (the constant definition's fallback default), line 14648 (defensive `typeof EXAM_PASS_SCORE === 'number' ? EXAM_PASS_SCORE : 720` — correct pattern), and ~8 comments (no functional impact). 1 UAT guard MIGRATED: v4.54.3 `passed = scaled >= 720` → `passed = scaled >= EXAM_PASS_SCORE` (tracks the new cert-aware pattern). 3 new UAT tombstones: finish() must not hardcode 720 in verdict/gap; submitExam result msg must not hardcode 720; milestone descs must not hardcode 720 (prevents regression). ## CSS Theme System
Dark theme in `:root`, light theme in `[data-theme="light"]`. Key variables: `--bg`, `--surface`, `--accent`, `--text`, `--green`, `--red`, `--yellow`. Toggle via `toggleTheme()`.

## Project Boards (two separate trackers)
Two Kanban boards, each with distinct purpose — never mix them.

### Bug / Tech Debt tracker
- [Board #1](https://github.com/users/oremosu98/projects/1) — bugs and tech debt only
- Labels: `bug`, `tech-debt`
- Priority field: 🔴 High, 🟡 Medium, 🟢 Low / Quick Win
- `tests/tech-debt.js` runs in CI on every push — breaches auto-create issues with `tech-debt` + `priority: medium` labels, added to board in Backlog
- Auto-reported bugs get `bug` + `priority: high` labels, added to board in Backlog
- Weekly cadence (post-2026-04-18 Option A): **Tuesdays** for bugs, **Thursdays** for tech debt
- Tighten tech debt thresholds as debt is paid down

### Feature Ideas tracker
- [Board #2](https://github.com/users/oremosu98/projects/2) — future feature candidates only
- Label: `feature-idea` (purple)
- Priority field: 🔥 Must Have, ⭐ Should Have, 💡 Nice to Have, 🧊 Someday
- Effort field: XS / S / M / L / XL
- Tie-in field: Cert SaaS Vision / Quiz App Only / Both
- Tied to product vision doc at `~/Desktop/Dev Projects/product-vision/PRODUCT-VISION.md`
- Weekly cadence (post-2026-04-18 Option A): **Mondays + Wednesdays + Fridays** for shipping features — pull a `🔥 Must Have` or `⭐ Should Have`, ship end-to-end same day (code → UAT → Chrome MCP verify → version bump → CLAUDE.md row → push → CI green). Don't start anything that can't realistically ship the same day; split larger ideas across multiple feature-day slots.
- Promote to Board #1 (as `tech-debt` or regular work) only when actually scheduled

### Routing rules
- Broken behavior / regression / crash → Board #1 with `bug`
- Code smell / duplication / architecture → Board #1 with `tech-debt`
- New capability / UX enhancement / product direction → Board #2 with `feature-idea`
- Every item is an individual issue — no master checklists

### `saas-gated` convention
A cross-board label marking items **frozen until the SaaS pivot triggers**. Exists on both Board #1 (tech-debt items that only pay off at scale, e.g. module split) and Board #2 (features that assume paid users, e.g. entitlements). **Do not pull a `saas-gated` issue without explicit pivot direction.** Full current list: see the *Conventions → `saas-gated` Label* section above.

### Auto-add to boards
- `.github/workflows/auto-add-to-board.yml` listens for `issues.opened/labeled/reopened` and routes via GraphQL: `tech-debt`/`bug` → Board #1, `feature-idea` → Board #2
- Requires repo secret `PROJECT_TOKEN` (a PAT with `project` scope) — without it the GraphQL `addProjectV2ItemById` call fails because the default `GITHUB_TOKEN` does not carry the `project` scope

### Auto-archive closed issues (JIRA-style "done disappears")
- `.github/workflows/auto-archive-done.yml` listens for `issues.closed` and calls `archiveProjectV2Item` on every board that contains the issue
- Uses the `issue.projectItems` reverse-lookup so it works for any board the issue is on (not hardcoded to Board #1 or #2)
- Archived items still exist in the board's **Archive** section — nothing is deleted, just hidden from the default view
- Same `PROJECT_TOKEN` secret as auto-add; falls back to `GITHUB_TOKEN` if unset (which will fail with insufficient scopes — that's intentional so the issue surfaces loudly)

### Board #2 (Feature Ideas) custom fields
- **Epic** (single-select, 6 options): 🟣 Study Technique · 🔵 Focus & ADHD · 🟠 Exam Day · 🟢 Memorization · 🟡 Port Drill · 🩷 UX Polish — use board Group-by to get JIRA-style swimlanes
- **Priority** (4 tiers): 🔥 Must Have · ⭐ Should Have · 💡 Nice to Have · 🧊 Someday
- **Effort** (5 tiers): XS (<1 day) · S · M · L · XL
- **Tie-in**: Cert SaaS Vision · Quiz App Only · Both
- Every feature-idea issue also carries a matching `epic:*` label for list-view filtering (redundant by design — the label survives even if the board is rebuilt)

## Weekly Cadence

**Option A** — adopted 2026-04-18 when roadmap queue hit 8 phases (ACL v2 + TB v2). Three feature-days + two hygiene days so the codebase stays shippable.

| Day | Lane |
|---|---|
| **Mon** | Feature ship (Board #2). Fresh-week energy → fits bigger scopes |
| **Tue** | Bug fixes (Board #1, `bug`) |
| **Wed** | Feature ship (Board #2) |
| **Thu** | Tech debt (Board #1, `tech-debt`; auto-sweep scheduled) |
| **Fri** | Feature ship (Board #2). Traditionally the signature ship |

Each feature-day is end-to-end: code → UAT → Chrome MCP verify → bump → CLAUDE.md row → push → CI green. Don't start anything that can't ship the same day. Weekend stays off — rest + N10-009 study.

**Scaling rules**: drop Wed back to rest when queue <4. Consider a 4th feature-day (Option B) only if queue >12 AND bandwidth is genuinely there. Pre-2026-04-18 cadence was Fri-only — fine through v4.52.0, compressed when the pipeline grew.

## Common Gotchas

**Code shape**
- The `pick()` function targets `#options .option` — CLI sim diagnosis MCQ must be inside `#options` div
- Topology scoring uses `correctPlacements` object mapping device→zone name (exact string match)
- Exam answers init must include `cliRan: [], topoState: {}` for PBQ types
- `hasAnswer` checks must include `Object.keys(a.topoState || {}).length > 0`
- `setQuestionText(el, raw)` order is **escape-THEN-highlight** (`escHtml` → `highlightExamKeywords` → `innerHTML`). Reversing it is an XSS hole since question text is AI-generated.
- The `_fnBody(src, name)` helper used by UAT extracts function bodies via brace-depth walking. **Prefix-match trap**: `tbShowCoach` will match `tbShowCoachModalLoading`. When writing UAT for a function, pick a name that's either unique or specify the exact suffix.

**Testing**
- Don't tune `validateQuestions()` without running `node tests/validation-audit.js` first — the `MIN_CATCH_RATE = 60` / `MAX_FP_RATE = 0` floor is CI-enforced inside UAT
- Don't pull `saas-gated` items (see Conventions list) without explicit pivot direction
- `tests/uat.js` prefers behavioral smoke over structural; see Testing Philosophy

**Deploy**
- Service worker cache name must be bumped on every deploy or users get stale files — use `scripts/bump-version.js`, never hand-edit partial
- Vercel CLI requires nvm path export: `export PATH="$HOME/.nvm/versions/node/v20.20.2/bin:$PATH"`
- If you're tempted to `vercel --prod` without committing, **commit and push immediately after** — git↔prod drift cost us 6 versions (v4.39→v4.43.1) before it got caught
- Branch protection on `main` requires the "UAT + Playwright" status check; admin bypass works but defeats the point — only use for real emergencies

**Infra**
- `PROJECT_TOKEN` repo secret is a PAT with `project` scope (not the default `GITHUB_TOKEN`). Powers both `auto-add-to-board.yml` and `auto-archive-done.yml`. If rotated, update in GitHub repo secrets or both workflows fail loud.
- `deploy-verification.yml` runs post-deploy against the public URL — legit failures mean prod is broken; stale-cache failures mean give CDN a minute and re-run.
- When UAT fails mid-session, check `tests/validation-audit.js` first — a change to `validateQuestions()`, the GT tables, or the prompt can trip the regression gate without any UAT-level error being obvious.

---

## Post-deploy verification (always run after ship)

Headless UAT and Playwright pass while real users see broken UI — happened 7 times across v6.5.0 → v6.5.7. After any feature or fix lands on `main` and the Deploy Verification workflow reports success, **drive the live prod URL in a real browser before claiming done**.

### Workflow

1. **Cache-bust navigate** — open the prod URL with a `?_cb=<version>` query so the Service Worker cache is bypassed and you see the freshly-deployed code.
   - Main app: `https://networkplus.certanvil.com/?cert=netplus&_cb=<ver>`
   - Use the Chrome MCP tools (`mcp__Claude_in_Chrome__*`).

2. **Reproduce the user's exact click path** — don't shortcut via JS calls. If the feature ships behind a mode pill / button / scenario picker, click through it the way a user would (using `MouseEvent` dispatch when `.click()` doesn't trigger handlers).

3. **Measure DOM rects + computed styles, not just internal state**:
   - Canvas / panel widths and heights (a 138px-tall canvas means layout is broken even if state looks correct)
   - `getComputedStyle()` for text/background colors on the actual elements (catches theme-token bugs that look fine in mockups)
   - `position`, `transform`, `display` on new rail panels (catches CSS Grid collisions)
   - Element visibility via `offsetParent !== null` + bounding-rect inside the viewport

4. **Walk through the full user flow end-to-end** — first interaction, advance, completion, exit, reload. Not just the first click.

5. **Only then claim "shipped + verified".** If anything looks off, ship a hotfix before signing off — don't wait for the user to find it.

### Skip the verification only when

- The change is purely backend / data / docs with no user-facing surface
- The change is behind a feature flag that's off in prod

### Why this rule exists

Pre-v6.5.x every CI pass was treated as "shipped". But UAT regex-tests source strings and Playwright runs fresh navigations — both miss live-interaction layout bugs, theme-mismatched colors, viewport state carry-over, and CSS Grid collisions. Every one of v6.5.1 → v6.5.7 was a bug the user found by clicking in their real browser that an automated post-deploy visual check would have caught.
